Grand Prix Oakland Last Chance Trial 4-0 Decklists
==================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on January 5, 2019 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20211024110319im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Colette LeRoux











Congratulations to all the winners of the Last Chance Trials held on Friday of GP Oakland! In true Modern form, competitors brought a wide selection of archetypes to battle. Here is a selection of decklists representing the myriad of archetypes that took down their pods:
